 Gadkari said that Gowda did a very good job as the chief minister, and there are no complaints of corruption against him
 gadakari ne bataaya ki party netaa arun jetali or rajnath sih somvaar ko bengaluru jaakar rajya ke party netritv se baat karenge
 After that there will be a meeting of party mlas, after which Sadanand Gowda and Shettar will meet the Governor
 gauda kii vidaai kii vajah rajya ke purv mukhyamantri vies yediurppa kii jid ko mana ja rahaa he
 Shettar will be the third BJP Chief Minister of the state since 2008
 vahiin dilli pahunche gauda ne karnataka bhawan main patrakaron se kaha ki unhone party ke ek aagyaakaari sipaahi kii tarah pad kaa tyaag kar diya he
 He said that the central leadership of the party made him aware that the change in the leadership of the state was being done for some political reasons, then he accepted it
 bhaajapa sutron ke mutabik gauda ko rajyasabha kaa sadsy banaaya jayega
 He was a member of the Lok Sabha before becoming Chief Minister
 mukhyamantri ke naam ke liye shettar ke naam kii ghoshnaa ke saath hi bengaluru se 400 kilometre dur unke shahar hubli main jashn kaa maahaul kaayam ho gaya, jabaki gauda ke ilaake, tateey karnataka main maayusi chaa gai
 a BJP Legislature Party meeting will be held in Bengaluru on Monday, in which Shettar will be formally elected as the leader of the Legislature Party to meet Governor HR Bhardwaj to stake claim to form the government
 vahiin party hai kaman ko dilli main apana istipha saunpkar bengaluru waapas pahunche gauda kaa hawaii adde par unke samarthakon ne joardaar swaagat kiya
 Gowda took over as Chief Minister on August 4 last year, and he has not been able to complete even one year of his rule
 gauratlab he ki shuukravaar ko shettar sahit rajya mantrimandal ke aath sadasyon ne mukhyamantri badalane kii maang ko lekar apana istipha de diya tha
 Only after this did the central leadership decide to make Shettar the chief minister
 congress ne karnataka main bhaajapa dwaara netritv main kiye ja rahe badlaav ko 'bhrashtachar kii jeet' bataaya
 The comments congress mahasachiv bike hariprasad ne kaha, "yah bhaajapa ke bhrashtachar kii jeet he
 
 bhrasht log gauda ke khilaaf the
 BJP leaders will be exposed
 " At the same time, JD (U) President Sharad Yadav said that Gowda was martyred for the presidential election
 unhone kaha, "yadi raashtrapati chunaav nahin hota to unhen istipha nahin dena padataa
 " bhaajapa ke is faisle par congress or bhaajapa ke sahyogi janata dal (united) ne tikhi pratikriya di he
 While the Congress has called the change in leadership a 'victory for corruption', the JD (U) has said that Gowda has been 'martyred' for the presidential election
 gadakari ne yahaan apane awaas ke baahar patrakaron se kaha ki karnataka ke taaja raajnneetik halaat ko dekhte hue gauda ne unhen bataaya he ki vah rajya ke mukhyamantri pad se istipha de rahe hai
 Gadkari said, "looking at the future of Karnataka, we have decided to hand over the reins of the state to Jagdish Shettar
 " At the same time, Gadkari informed that Gowda will be given new responsibilities at the central and state level
 rajya main jari raajnneetik sankat ke bich sadanand gauda shanivaar ko dilli aae, or unhone laalkrishna adwani, sushamaa swaraj, arun jetali or anant kumaar jaise party ke kendriya netaaon se mulaakaat kii
 He met Gadkari on Sunday morning
 gadakari ne kaha ki gauda ne mukhyamantri ke taur par kaaphi acha kaam kiya, or unke khilaaf bhrashtachar kii koi shikaayat nahin he
 Gadkari said that party leaders Arun Jaitley and Rajnath Singh will go to Bangalore on Monday to talk to the state's party leadership
 uske baad party vidhayakon kii baithak hogi, jiske baad sadanand gauda or shettar rajyapal se mulaakaat karenge
 Gowda's departure is believed to be due to the insistence of former state Chief Minister VS Yeddyurappa
 shettar, 2008 se rajya main satta main ai bhaajapa ke tisare mukhyamantri honge
 Gowda, who arrived in Delhi, told reporters at the Karnataka Bhavan that he had relinquished his post as an obedient soldier of the party
 unhone kaha ki party ke kendriya netritv ne unhen avgat karaayaa ki kuch raajnneetik kaarnon se rajya ke netritv main badlaav kiya ja rahaa he to unhone ise sweekaar kar liya
 According to BJP sources, Gowda will be made a member of the Rajya Sabha
 mukhyamantri banane se pehle vah loksabhaa sadsy the
 With the announcement of Shettar as the Chief Minister's name, there was a festive atmosphere in his hometown Hubli, 400 km from Bangalore, while desolation took place in Gowda's area, coastal Karnataka
 somvaar ko bengaluru main bhaajapa vidhayak dal kii baithak hogi, jisamen shettar ko aupchaarik rup se vidhayak dal kaa netaa chunaa jayega, taaki vah rajyapal echaar bharadwaj se milakar sarkaar banane kaa daawa pesh kar saken
 Gowda, who returned to Bengaluru by handing over his resignation to the party high command in Delhi, was strongly welcomed by his supporters at the airport
 gauda ne pichley saal chaar agast ko mukhyamantri kii kursi sanbhali thi, or vah apane shashan kaa ek saal bhi puraa nahin sake hai
 Significantly, on Friday, eight members of the state cabinet, including Shettar, tendered their resignations demanding change of chief minister
 iske baad hi kendriya netritv ne shettar ko mukhyamantri banane kaa faisla kiya
 The Congress termed the change being led by the BJP in Karnataka as a 'victory of corruption'
 tippaniyan Congress General Secretary BK Hariprasad said, â€œthis is a victory for BJP corruption
 
 Corrupt people were against Gowda
 bhaajapa ke netaa benakaab honge
 " vahiin, jad (yu) ke adhyaksh sharad yadav ne kaha ki gauda ko raashtrapati chunaav ke liye shahid kiya gaya
 He said, "he would not have to resign if there were no presidential elections
 " Gadkari told reporters outside his residence here that Gowda had told him that he was resigning as the Chief Minister of the state, given the recent political situation in Karnataka
 gadakari ne kaha, "karnataka ke bhavishya ko dekhte hue hamane rajya kii bagdor jagadish shettar ko saunpane kaa faisla kiya he
 " saath hi gadakari ne bataaya ki gauda ko kendra or rajya str par nai jimmedaari saunpi jaaegi
